Panic Over Soaring Gold Prices in Shenyang 56

A dispatch from Shenyang reports that recently gold has become valuable and silver cheap, causing a drastic change in the economy. The market price of gold notes has risen sharply while the value of silver dollars has fallen. One hundred and twenty-five yuan in Feng Piao (Feng Piao are officially valued by the government at sixty yuan to one yuan) can only be exchanged for one yuan in gold notes. Harbin dollars can be exchanged at a rate of two yuan and twenty-five cents for one yuan in gold notes. Silver dollars can be exchanged at a rate of one yuan and ninety-six cents for one yuan in gold notes. This has a direct or indirect and extremely large impact on various commercial firms and tax revenues in the province. The details are as follows:

(1) Residents: With the soaring price of gold, merchants selling imported goods priced in gold and Chinese goods priced in silver have taken the opportunity to raise prices. Even local products unrelated to the price of gold, such as flour, sorghum, millet, bean oil, and all daily food and supplies, have increased dramatically. Residents are suffering from the high cost of living and are now facing this difficult situation, complaining incessantly. Residents in the city, who live on Chinese territory and whose rent and daily expenses are based on Chinese currency, are only slightly affected. However, residents living in the Japanese-controlled area are greatly affected, as rent has always been very high. A typical, substandard room costs nine yuan in gold notes. Now that the price of gold has risen to more than double the value of silver dollars, each room costs the equivalent of eighteen silver dollars. Middle and lower-class families, such as small vendors and craftsmen, feel that their hard-earned silver dollars cannot afford the rent calculated in gold notes. Recently, a group of tenants jointly petitioned the landlord, asking for a slight reduction. The landlord, a Japanese person, initially refused, but after much pleading, he reduced the rent by seven fen per yuan, meaning a nine-yuan gold note rent was reduced by six jiao and three fen. Even with this reduction, the rent has still invisibly increased to such an extent. Other clothing and daily necessities, especially Japanese goods, are purchased at gold note prices, resulting in significant losses.

(2) Business Sector: All goods purchased by stores that are normally priced in gold notes have suffered greatly. Some stores with limited capital are temporarily unable to repay their debts to Japanese merchants. Others have suffered such heavy losses that they are insolvent and have absconded.

(3) Government: The severe losses suffered by businesses in various counties make it difficult for them to sustain operations, leading to an invisible shutdown. As a result, tax collection agencies have no revenue. According to sources in the Finance Department, the tax revenue of various county tax bureaus in May was mostly only 30% of the required quota, a shortfall of 70%. Concerned about performance evaluations, they have requested the Finance Department to review the situation and revise the quotas. The department is currently considering the matter.

(4) Press: Because there are no large-scale paper mills in the Northeast, most of the paper used is purchased from Japan and priced in gold notes, which has increased several times over. As a result, one or two businesses have closed down, while four or five are struggling to survive under financial pressure. One has shortened the length of its publications to maintain the status quo. Currently, Zhang Xueliang, the Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast, has issued an order to the governments of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang provinces to quickly find ways to maintain financial stability and assist businesses, strictly prohibiting the export of cash. The General Chamber of Commerce is also concerned that the difficulties faced by businesses will lead to widespread closures, and has held repeated meetings to discuss solutions and request assistance from the provincial government. Zang Shiyi, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, recently convened a meeting with the president of the Chamber of Commerce, the general manager of the official silver bureau of the three eastern provinces, and leaders in the banking industry to discuss relief measures. The following resolutions were made: (1) Appropriately reduce taxes and levies. (2) Order various banks to provide loans. The lending method is that the official bank will prepare 3 million yuan, guaranteed by the local chamber of commerce, to lend to various businesses, but not more than 500 yuan per business. At the same time, the provincial government will issue an order to the magistrates of 58 counties, including Shenyang, to work with the public security bureaus and county chambers of commerce to quickly stabilize prices in order to maintain people's livelihoods and the market. (June 11th)

Baker's Report on the Shaanxi Famine 57

Baker, the Director of Relief Operations for the China International Famine Relief Commission, has returned to Beijing after inspecting the famine in Shaanxi. His report states that "burial teams in Xi'an City must patrol the streets twice a day," illustrating the severity of the disaster. Baker recently sent a letter to the Shanghai office of the United China Relief Association in the United States, describing the famine in great detail. The original text is translated as follows:

"In the Xi'an Plain area, which is 100 miles long and averages 20-30 miles wide, the wheat and millet are in good condition. Only 5% of the area within Sanyuan County offers hope, and west of that, there is no hope at all. The new grain in Xi'an is now on the market, but the market price is still ten times higher than usual. This shows that the new grain on the market cannot lower the price of grain. The 5 million people in Shaanxi Province need 4,000 tons of grain every day. This wheat harvest will yield at most 200,000 tons, which is only enough for 50 days. Therefore, grain still needs to be imported from other provinces to make up for the shortfall. Our association (Famine Relief Commission) has transported a total of 2,000 tons of relief grain to Shaanxi, making every effort and paying transportation costs several times higher than the price of the grain to get it into Shaanxi. However, the needs of the disaster area are enormous, and our relief grain is like a drop in the ocean, unable to provide widespread relief. Currently, tens of thousands of people are relying on begging for a living, or eating rotten food, or eating at porridge kitchens. Most can barely survive the hot summer, but once winter comes or the porridge kitchens close, they will still die of starvation. These people have no land, and even if Xi'an has a good harvest, they will not be able to enjoy its benefits. They are also physically weak, unable to work, and have no chance of getting food. I have urged my colleagues to gather disaster victims begging on the streets who have no opium addiction and whose bodies are not yet weak, and to accommodate them in porridge kitchens. In the first week, they are given one jin of grain per day, and in the second week, it is increased to one and a half jin to prevent the disaster victims from dying from bloating after prolonged starvation due to excessive feeding. In the third week, they will recover their strength and can be assigned to road work, with sufficient rations provided according to their work. This will maintain their livelihood until after the autumn harvest. These disaster victims are marked with symbols for identification. After being accommodated, if they are found to be begging again or absconding with tools, they will be handed over to the authorities for severe punishment. Although we are actively engaged in famine relief in Shaanxi, a famine in Shaanxi is still feared to be unavoidable. Landlords and laborers with land to cultivate can hope to recover after the summer and autumn harvests, but disaster victims who are poor, landless, and physically weak still need relief. Moreover, because these people usually eat rotten food, they will inevitably suffer from dysentery in the summer, and even more will die in the cold winter. In short, whether to find ways to help these disaster victims regain their health or to let them languish and die in the harsh winter depends on what our conscience dictates."

Guangdong Province

Twists and Turns in the Reorganization of Merchant Organizations 58

A dispatch from Guangzhou reports that the method for reorganizing merchant organizations throughout the province was previously determined by the Training Department of the Provincial Party Headquarters. Cheng Shaojie was appointed as the chairman of the reorganization committee of the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, and each of the old and new federations of commerce designated thirteen members to be committee members. The first meeting was held on the 27th of last month, and it was decided to take over the old and new federations of commerce on a fixed date and draft the reorganization charter. Subsequently, Chen Mingshu, the Minister of the Training Department of the Provincial Party Headquarters, believed that the number of members of the reorganization committee was too large and that it would be inconvenient for organization and operation, and that it was slightly different from the Guangzhou merchant organization reorganization method recently instructed by the Central Committee's Municipal Party Headquarters. In order to unify the work steps, the reorganization committee was ordered to stop its progress, and its first resolution was also ordered to be cancelled. The reorganization method was re-established and renamed the Guangdong Provincial Merchant Organization Guidance Committee, designated to act on behalf of the Provincial Federation of Commerce and the Provincial Association of Commerce, and to prepare for the formal establishment of the Provincial Federation of Commerce. Except for the Provincial Association of Commerce, which had been taken over by the Party Headquarters and should be handed over, the old and new federations of commerce should be taken over by the Guidance Committee. Matters that cannot be resolved during the working period may be submitted to the Provincial Training Department for guidance, and the working time is stipulated to be four months. The expenses are raised by the old and new federations of commerce, and the number of committee members is set at nine. Three people are recommended by the old and new federations of commerce from the previous thirteen people, and another three people are added by the Party Headquarters from the former members of the Provincial Association of Commerce, making a total of nine people. The above-mentioned committee members are requested by the Provincial Training Department to be appointed by the Provincial Committee. A meeting was scheduled for the 9th of this month to convene thirteen members from the old and new federations of commerce at the Provincial Party Headquarters to elect three members from each committee as attending members. However, it was found that only four people from the new federation of commerce attended that day, which was less than the legal number, and the meeting could not be held. According to the opinions of the members of the new federation of commerce, the reorganization method was not perfect. It was said that the Provincial Association of Commerce had been ordered to close down, and the old and new federations of commerce were merged and reorganized later. Now that the reorganization is being started, the Provincial Association of Commerce itself no longer exists, so how can it be allowed for the members of the association to participate in it? Moreover, this reorganization of the Provincial Federation of Commerce is being watched by the chambers of commerce in various regions. If the members of the Provincial Association of Commerce, which has been closed, are specially allowed to be reorganization guidance committee members, once this precedent is set, the disputes in the reorganization of the chambers of commerce in various regions in the future will be unimaginable. Committee members Liang Yucai and others have already put forward their opinions requesting that the proposal to add three former members of the Provincial Association of Commerce as members of the organization guidance committee be cancelled. If the Provincial Party Headquarters must allow members of the association to be committee members, the proposal can be changed to participate in the name of the Party Headquarters so that it does not contradict the case that the Provincial Association of Commerce has been closed and avoid disputes in the reorganization of the name of the chamber of commerce in the future. Otherwise, if the chambers of commerce in various regions use the participation of the Provincial Association of Commerce in the reorganization of the Provincial Federation of Commerce as a basis, how can the disputes be easily resolved? Therefore, the election of committee members to form the Provincial Federation of Commerce Guidance Committee at the Party Headquarters on the 9th was suspended again. The Training Department of the Provincial Party Headquarters believes that there is no way to resolve it, and intends to ask the Minister of Training, Chen Mingshu, for instructions before submitting it to the Provincial Executive Committee for review. (11th)

After the Transfer of Xiang Hanping's Troops to Chaozhou and Shantou 59

A dispatch from Shantou reports that the 62nd Division of Xiang Hanping has been transferred to Chaozhou and Shantou to garrison. Zhang Da's brigade and Wu Jianxiong's regiment are stationed in Meixian, Li Zhenliang's regiment is stationed in Xingning in the upper reaches of the Meijiang River, and Zhang Ruigui's brigade is stationed in various coastal counties of Chaozhou and Shantou. The headquarters of the 62nd Division has been moved to Shantou. Xiang Hanping himself is recuperating in the province due to a minor illness and has not yet arrived in Shantou. After the completion of the transfer of Xiang's division, Zheng Zichun's 15th regiment of the 8th Brigade of the 61st Division arrived in Shantou on the 11th and returned to the province by Anli round. Zhang Zhiying's Fourth Independent Regiment was ordered by Chen Jitang on the 10th to return to the province. The train was extremely busy transporting troops yesterday and stopped taking passengers. The local communists in various forts of Meixian in the upper reaches of the Han River are extremely rampant. According to news from Meixian, after Zhu De and Mao Zedong retreated to Xunwu and Wuping, the local militia jointly counterattacked the county seat and recaptured it on the 6th. Chen Xuesheng, the puppet county chairman, was captured alive and shot dead by the militia in Bachih. Currently, various villages in Pingyuan are as stable as usual, and the communist soldiers followed Zhu De and Mao Zedong and fled to the border of Jiangxi in the Niudouguang and Huangshe areas. On the 7th of this month, the local communists in Shikeng, Meixian, coerced more than 1,000 women and children to surround and rob the Luo Junkeng and Ling Zeng families in Shixia, burning down more than a dozen houses, looting and killing civilians, and forcing people to join the association. The county magistrate of Meixian, upon hearing the report, has dispatched a team to search and suppress the bandits in Longhuwei. Also, on the 5th, 500 bandits from Xiyang Inner Mountain looted the Huang family in Longkeng, the hometown of Huang Chengdian, the battalion commander of the special service battalion, completely looting rice, grain, livestock, etc., and kidnapping seven Huang men and six women. Huang Chengdian immediately printed and distributed a notice to the people of Inner Mountain, limiting them to release the kidnapped people and return the rice, grain, and livestock within three days. When the bandits ignored him, Huang decided to lead a team to suppress them on the 8th. Other villages, such as the Xiong family in Pankeng and villages ten miles outside the city, are constantly harassed by bandits, and the people have moved away. Shops in the Shekeng and Changsha markets have closed down and are now guarded by troops to cut off the bandits' food supply in the mountains.

In Dapu County, due to the continuous transfer of troops, the communist gangs Deng Yi and Deng Yigang and others revolted again in Dachan and Mujiiao villages, causing a shock in Baihou. The Shiyun District urgently telegraphed Dapu County for help. It was found that the Deng bandits had invaded Gaobei and Shiyun districts from Lixia Dam last month, and more than 200 guns were lost by the police. This month, they invaded again from Zhongkeng to Gucun, Zuobi, and Yangmen, causing significant losses. Gucun is only five miles away from Dapu City. Dapu is surrounded by bandits, all industries have been abandoned, schools have been closed, and children have been deprived of education. Only the Sanhe and Tongren districts are relatively stable. (12th)

Sudden Turmoil at the Zhongyuan Textile Mill in Qingdao 60

Seven workers arrested by the Public Security Bureau for alleged involvement in a plot to disrupt factory operations

Workers surround police station and fire shots in protest

A dispatch from Qingdao reports that the six yarn factories established by the Japanese in Sifang and Cangkou last year experienced a storm that shut down production for half a year. After mediation by all parties, operations were restored. At that time, a number of workers deemed undesirable by the Japanese were laid off, and the factories resumed work. Many of these unemployed workers were sent back to their hometowns with severance pay, but many remained in Qingdao. Recently, they have been used by reactionary elements and have secretly contacted workers at the Zhongyuan Textile Mill to plot disturbances. Someone recently reported this to the Municipal Government. To be cautious, the Municipal Government secretly ordered the Industrial and Commercial Association to investigate and report back before taking action. After receiving the order, the Industrial and Commercial Association, together with police officers from the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau in Cangkou, went to investigate. According to general rumors, there was indeed such a plan. The Municipal Government then ordered the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau to send personnel, along with police officers from the First Branch of the Cangkou Public Security Bureau, to arrest the seven leading workers around midnight on the 11th and send them to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. On the morning of the 12th, the remaining workers heard the news and sent more than 200 representatives to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government to request their release. When they failed to achieve their goal, the workers immediately held an emergency meeting and claimed that police officers from the First Branch of the Police station had been present during the investigation and arrest, and that the branch was the instigator. Without clarifying the situation, they went to the Cangkou Police station en masse, surrounded it, and fired several shots into the air. The police station also took strict precautions and fired shots into the air to intimidate them. Businesses in Cangkou, unaware of the situation, rushed to close their doors. After receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched a security team to suppress the situation, and the Naval Headquarters also sent marines to maintain order. Seventeen leading workers were arrested and the rest were dispersed. A storm was averted. It is reported that the workers held another meeting in the factory at 6:00 AM this morning and decided to continue working as usual. Representatives were sent to various party and government agencies to request bail for the arrested workers. The marines who were sent to Cangkou have already withdrawn to Qingdao, and a part of the security team and police officers from the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau are still maintaining order on the ground. It is still difficult to determine how this matter will be resolved. (June 13th)

Water Measurement by the Taihu Lake Conservancy Association 61

The Taihu Lake basin has flat terrain and crisscrossing rivers. The water flow situation is very complicated due to the inflow and outflow of lakes and the influence of tides from the Yangtze River. Over the years, the former Taihu Lake Conservancy Bureau and the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Project Office have set up stations at important locations in the basin to measure water flow more than once. After the reorganization and establishment of the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Commission, a dedicated surveying team was established to survey the flow of water from the outlet of Taihu Lake, which has been going on for more than half a year. Although considerable achievements have been made, it is still insufficient to only measure the outflow volume during the summer and autumn flood seasons. Therefore, the surveying and mapping section of the commission carefully planned and formulated a measurement method. It was decided that from the plum rain season to the end of the flood season, personnel will be dispatched to set up measurement stations at the inlets and outlets of Taihu Lake and related rivers. Recently, they have successively set off in eight teams stationed in Wuxi, Suzhou, Wujiang, Weiting, Wuxing, Jiapu, Dapu, Baidu and other places. There are nine measuring stations in total, located at Gaoqiao, Wangting in Wuxi, Hushu Pass, Likou, Mudu in Suzhou, Guajingkou, Beizha, Pingwang, Zhouxiang in Weiting, Daqiankou, Xiaomeikou in Wuxing, Jiapukou, Dapukou, Wuxikou, Baidukou, etc. Among them, there are six inlets and six outlets, and seven related rivers. In the future, the influence of Taihu Lake itself on the entire basin can be clearly understood based on the results of this measurement. Agricultural irrigation and shipping in the Taihu Lake basin are more developed than other places, which relies on the large area of ​​Taihu Lake to store water for support. However, in recent years, the issue of increasing siltation and reclaiming land from the lake has been advocated by the general public, but there is still no scientific research on the matter. The commission is aware of this, so even though the work is very complicated, it still makes efforts to organize it. In addition to sending technical personnel Lu Chuanyue, Zhuang Zemin, Lin Xiaofang, Hu Qingtao, Zhao Zuzhang, Hua Zhongwen, Zhou Rongjing, and Wang Dunren to set off separately, official letters were also sent to the governments of Wuxi, Wuxian, Wujiang, Wuxing, and Yixing counties to request local protection and assistance at any time to facilitate the progress of the survey.

Opinions of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining on Relief for the Unemployed 64

(Continued)

B. Matters relating to forestry

(1) Implement afforestation (Reasons) Our country has many barren mountains suitable for afforestation, and the afforestation technology is simple and the required capital is easy to raise. (Methods) Afforestation must be carried out by the government and the people in a practical cooperation, so that better effect can be achieved and more forest workers can be accommodated. The outline of the methods is as follows: Regarding the government side (1) Central: The central government can carry out afforestation directly on a scale that can be large or small. However, given the current financial difficulties, it does not seem appropriate to indulge in extravagance. The practical measures that can be taken are planned as follows: 1. Expand the scope of the Central Model Forest Area, increase the budget, and establish four state-owned afforestation farms. The locations should be near the Eastern Tombs of Hebei, Xusi near Suwan, Shaochen near Huguang, and near Guangxin in Eyu. 2. In addition to the annual increase in the budget for the Central Model Forest Area, the expenses for the remaining four state-owned afforestation farms should also be paid directly by the central government. Each site should have an initial establishment fee of 25,000 yuan, and the regular and temporary fees should be an average of 20,000 yuan per month. The total cost per year is about 1 million yuan. Together with the five central model forest areas, about 7,000 workers can be accommodated. (2) Provinces: The provinces must implement a forest area system to carry out afforestation. The central government should order each province to divide into several forest areas according to the province's mountains, rivers, and natural conditions, and carry out them separately. It is decided that each province will accommodate an average of 2,000 forest workers, and the whole country will be able to accommodate 50,000 unemployed people. (3) Counties: The afforestation matters of each county shall be handled by the provincial government. It is decided that each county will accommodate an average of 100 workers, and the whole country will be able to accommodate more than 200,000 unemployed people. In addition to the above three, the central government should issue an order to all water management agencies in the country to earnestly carry out the construction of security forests, and the plan should be formulated by the competent authorities themselves. Regarding the people: (1) Promote forestry cooperatives. The harvest period of the forest industry is long, and private capital is weak, so there are many who want to step back. Forestry cooperatives should be promoted to make up for this. At the same time, afforestation incentive regulations should be formulated to encourage the domestic middle class to invest in afforestation. This will not only benefit forestry but also have an effect on solving the problem of unemployed people in our country. It is a win-win situation. (2) Implement compulsory afforestation. This section should be formulated by the central government after the forest method is announced and then the provinces should properly determine the implementation measures of compulsory afforestation according to local conditions. If it can be effectively promoted, it can also accommodate many unemployed workers.

(2) Create a forest police (Reasons) Everyone knows that promoting forestry must first emphasize protection policies. Therefore, the methods of advanced European and American forestry countries should be imitated to organize forest police. This can not only provide for the unemployed but also ensure the safe development of forestry. (Methods) The central government should immediately establish a forest police officer training class for a period of three or six months. A part of the students should be selected and sent by the provinces, and a part should be directly selected by the central government. After graduation, the students sent by the provinces should return to their provinces to organize the forest police. The students selected by the central government should be assigned to various state-owned afforestation farms to handle forest police matters. The required expenses are at most only 20,000 to 30,000 yuan.

(3) Prepare for the establishment of forestry training institutes (Reasons) Our country's barren mountains are suitable for planting trees, but the local customs are closed and few know what forestry is. The central and provincial governments should widely establish forestry training institutes to promote forestry knowledge and accommodate a part of the unemployed people. (Methods) 1. The purpose of this training institute is to train personnel to guide on-site afforestation. In addition to teaching common sense of forestry, special attention should be paid to practice. The training period is temporarily set at half a year. 2. The training institute should be hosted by the central government, and it seems appropriate to set it up in Mount Lu, because Jiangxi is rich in forests and the location is very suitable. As for the provinces, the local situation is different, and the provinces should decide whether to set up one or multiple schools by themselves. 3. The cost of each school is two or three million yuan at most and one million yuan at least, and the organizing agency should decide by itself.

(4) Reward forestry product manufacturing industry (Reasons) Our country's forestry product manufacturing industry, such as charcoal, camphor, lacquer liquid, tung oil, etc., is either related to international trade or is an important consumer product in society. However, over the years, the government has not given encouragement, which has led to a decline. As a result, it is necessary to find ways to promote its development, so that on the one hand, it can accommodate a large number of workers, and on the other hand, it can develop the national economy. (Methods) 1. Formulate regulations on rewarding forestry product manufacturing. 2. Appropriately reduce the amount of tax. 3. Whenever transported by state-owned railways, the freight should be reduced appropriately. 4. The government should provide subsidies when necessary.

(5) Maintain the original logging company (Reasons) The logging area of ​​our country is the first in the three eastern provinces. According to recent surveys, there are more than a dozen companies in Jilin's Xingcai Huasen Changning Huangquan and Harbin's Hailin Zhongdong and Andong's Manxian Yalu River Logging Company with a capital of more than 20,000 yuan. In name, they are jointly operated by China and Japan, but in fact, they are all controlled by the Japanese. The two forestry companies, Tienun and Songjiang, which are jointly operated by our country's officials and merchants, have suffered losses for years due to the oppression of the Japanese. The impact is related to the unemployment problem of our country's people. Therefore, for the sake of the national economy and for the sake of the unemployed, the government should find ways to support them so that they can continue to develop. (Methods) 1. The central government should send personnel to thoroughly clear up the past operating conditions of the two companies. 2. Change the organization of the company. 3. Conclude a cooperative agreement with the local government. 4. The central government should pay 100,000 yuan in renovation fees.

The above methods regarding forestry are all based on the current situation and the practical feasibility. If they can be implemented one by one, about 300,000 workers can be accommodated. The expenses required by the central government are about 1.5 million yuan, and the expenses for the undertakings that should be handled by the provinces and counties should be the responsibility of the provinces and counties themselves. (To be continued)

Stamp Tax Inspectors Extort Money: At 12:00 PM on June 8th, Tang Qi and Qian, who claimed to be stamp tax inspectors, suddenly came to Huajiaqiao Town. They arrived at the Xinxin Rice Mill, Wang Wanshun, Hengxin, and other tobacco and paper stores one after another. Without asking for any reason, they broke into the counter and rummaged through boxes, inspecting the account books one by one, and taking away a copy of the previous year's account book. They intimidated the shop owners, falsely claiming that they would be immediately fined 50, 30, and 20 yuan, respectively, under the law because the stamp tax on the account books was sufficient, or because the stamp was missing, or because the stamp was too small. The shop owners repeatedly pleaded, and they settled for 7, 5, and 2 yuan, totaling 14 yuan. Suzhou 69

Stray Bullets Suddenly Enter Agricultural School: At 12:00 PM yesterday (the 16th), at the Suzhou Agricultural Vocational School outside the Chaimen Wai Xiajin Bridge, students in the second year of the preparatory course were in class when three stray bullets suddenly flew into the classroom from outside, penetrated the window, and hit students Zhang Hengde (15 years old, from Jiading) in the right finger, Zhou Zhiang (19 years old, from Yixing) in the right upper arm, and Chen Yaolin (17 years old, from Danyang) in the left hand. The entire school was in panic, scrambling to run downstairs. At the same time, the school authorities sent the three injured students to Suyong Hospital for treatment. Zhang and Zhou were hospitalized, while Chen returned to school after dressing the wound. Afterwards, Principal Liao Jianan immediately reported the incident to the police district and requested a thorough investigation. Director Min of the Tu District led the police to investigate and found two pistol bullets in the ceiling of the second-year classroom. There were also bullet holes in the board. Upon inspection, it was determined that the bullet holes were caused by bullets fired from the direction of the Liuyuan Road on the south side. It was impossible to trace who fired the gun at that time. In addition to immediately dispatching police to conduct a thorough investigation to clarify the truth, he immediately reported the matter to the Public Security Bureau for review and handling. The entire student body of 105 students in the second academy has now put forward two solutions in writing to the principal, requesting permission to (1) immediately suspend classes for safety, and (2) move the painting to ensure future methods. Principal Liao is currently considering this matter.

Soldier Responsible for Incident Executed: More than 300 wounded soldiers stationed in Suzhou went to the county government on the afternoon of the 15th to demand awards and seize the guns of the county police team, and attempted to release prisoners from the Third Blue Prison branch. Fortunately, the 1st Regiment of the Garrison Brigade sent a team to suppress them. His life is in danger. Ying Zhongqin and Zhu Desheng, two of the ringleaders, were captured on the spot. Shi Juemin, the regimental commander of the garrison, confirmed that Zhou Heyan, a rapist who had escaped from the Third Prison branch during the chaos (31 years old, from Wuxian, a carpenter, sentenced to five years and two months), had escaped. The entire city was closed at the time, and a temporary curfew was announced. Military and police authorities sent telegrams to the province and Beijing for instructions. Shi Juemin, the regimental commander of the garrison, received a telegram at noon yesterday (the 16th) ordering the execution of the two wounded soldiers, Ying and Zhu, on the spot. Ying Zhongqin and Zhu Desheng were immediately escorted to the front of the county government and executed by firing squad.

Progress on Planning the Circum-Lake Highway: Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, believes that bandits are rampant in the areas along the lake in the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and residents cannot sleep peacefully. Although the central government has sent troops to suppress them, the root causes have not been eradicated and the aftermath is worrying. It is planned that they will set off for surveying immediately and then nail the central stakes. Fearing that the residents would misunderstand, it has been reported to the county government to issue a notice and order the district chiefs of each district along the lake to assist at any time to facilitate the progress.

Due to transfer issues during his tenure in Wu County, he came to Changzhou on the 15th to discuss everything with the current Chief of the Public Security Bureau, Yin Peng, and explained the process of the public report fee and other items he handled, and paid all the money that should be handed over in time. He will return to Jiangdu soon.

Changshu 72

Robbery Criminal Qian Axing Executed: Qian Axing (also known as Hu Wangxing) from Youdun, outside the South Gate, successively robbed five families, including Zhang Jin's family in Pujiagang, Wang Genyun's family in Hujingdi, and Lu Genfu's two families in Tangxibang, and injured two victims last spring. Zhu Shunqing, the captain of the Public Security Bureau's detective team, went to Shanghai to purchase the same eye line and arrested Qian Axing at the Shanghai-Ningbo Railway Station and sent him back to Changzhou. He was interrogated by the county government and confessed to being involved in robberies and according to the victims Lu Genfu and others, it was confirmed that Tan County Chief was approved by the provincial government on the 14th to sentence him to death. Secretary Jin, acting County Chief, signed and提 Qian Axing to the court at 6 PM to verify his identity, and escorted him to the execution ground in the North Gate to execute him by firing squad.

Fengxian 73

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Fang Sixteen: Although robbery cases have been emerging one after another in the western countryside of the county, the occurrence of kidnapping is still a first. According to reports, the farmer Lu Caigen's family in the village was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits after the guests left after a funeral. The bandits fired shots in the village to intimidate, and guarded the surrounding neighbors. Then, they rushed into the house to rob. However, the Lu family had been robbed twice and had little possessions. Because the bandits were not satisfied with what they got, they kidnapped his nine-year-old son, Ahe, before leaving. After the incident, the captains of the two bureaus of Yang and Li, stationed in the village, investigated and found that the bandits came and went by land, and then took their small boat to the southwest through a small port and fled. Based on their familiarity with the route and the way out, it can be determined that they were the same bandits who were not caught in the previous robbery case. The County Public Security Bureau has sent Inspector Chen Jinfang to investigate and set a deadline of two weeks to solve the case.

Nantong 74

Jiangbei Suppression of Bandits and Military Police Distribution: The nine counties of Tong, Ru, and others in Jiangbei are currently carrying out a major suppression of bandits. Li Changjiang, the temporary commander of the suppression of bandits, specifically distributed the military and police forces in the area. The four battalions of the provincial defense army, combined with two battalions of the national army's five divisions and local police forces and security regiments, have a strength of more than 5,000 people. Hu Xiangzao, Yu Shimei, Zhou Junbo, and the Qin family are responsible for Tonghai Qi, and Yang Weidong and Yang Chun are responsible for Yan.

Rear Wounded Soldiers Hospital Designated to Be Set Up in Nantong: A preparatory office has been set up for the Rear Wounded Soldiers Hospital and is jointly managed by the General Chamber of Commerce of Tongchonghaitai. The site of the hospital has been designated in Xiaoying, west of the city, and is currently being renovated.

Yangzhou 76

Huojiaqiao Robbed by Bandits: Huojiaqiao in the county was robbed by dozens of bandits armed with torches on the night of the 13th. They first went to the town and confiscated the guns of the security regiment, and then began to rob. They robbed six wealthy families in the town, including Wang San and a newly opened cloth store, and claimed that they had to take Wang San's son away. At the same time, when the Dada Company's large ship from Shanghai arrived at the town and passengers disembarked, they were all searched. It is reported that the losses in this battle were huge.

The Chief Culprit of the Huojia Road Incident in Yangzhou Was Arrested: It was reported that the county government received an order from the hall to strictly arrest the chief culprit in the Huojia Road roadwork incident in the county, which caused injuries to officials of the Construction Bureau. It is now heard that County Chief Chen found that Xia Guohuai of the Huanjiaqiao section of the road was the main criminal in this case and secretly ordered the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau of the battalion to immediately arrest Xia. After receiving the order, the director of the bureau immediately went and lured Xia to the city and handed him over to the county.

Explosives Explosion Injured Many People: There must be a race meeting in Daqiao Town in the county every year on the 18th day of the fifth lunar month, and the various explosive stores will also benefit three times from the market. A certain explosive store diagonally opposite the Public Security Bureau of the town accidentally caught fire, causing an explosion of explosives. The shop injured four people. Three of them were seriously injured and may be in danger of life after being sent to the hospital for treatment, and the remaining one is not in danger.

Jiangyin 77

Exploiting Labor Strikes to Create Extraneous Problems: On May 30th, exploiting the wage increase demands of workers in the spinning mill, a labor strike occurred. Labor representatives Ren Ruisheng and Li Jinshan were detained by the Public Security Bureau. After the resumption of work, the factory fired more than 40 male and female workers who participated in the strike. After investigation by the Public Security Bureau and according to the factory, a small box of ammunition, totaling 500 rounds, was found in the lamp room, indicating that they had illegally hidden military fire and violated the criminal law. The two were sent to the county government, but both denied the location of the ammunition. Yang Cheng, a trial judge, ordered them to be sent to the High Court for interrogation. At the same time, the county government ordered Public Security Bureau Chief Li to go to the yarn factory yesterday (the 15th) to investigate the source of the ammunition. According to worker Jiang Shunjin in the engine room, the bullets were found in a sack on the shelf in the repair shop and in a foreign oil tank. Zhu Yunwu and others saw it on the spot. Chief Li reported the results to the county for handling. There is still no specific plan for the dismissed workers to demand reinstatement.

Murderers Appeal for Interrogation: The case of Tao Shizhong of Zhouzhuang Township killing Feng A'er has been appealed to the High Court. The court will open on the afternoon of the 17th. The court ordered the county to dispatch Wu Bowen and other bailiffs to Suzhou today (16th) to extradite five defendants including Zhu Molang, Zhu Sanlang, Gao Amo, Gao Afu, and Jiang Zhouqing, and ten parties including Feng Yisheng to appear in court. The court also ordered that three counter-revolutionaries Liu Pinzhang, Gu Zengdao, and Pan Genquan be judged innocent, except that Gu Zengdao was involved in the Tienzhuang theft case and ordered him to be sent to Fushu County for review. Pan Genquan was sentenced to 20 years in prison for robbery and has not been fully executed. Liu Pinzhang had a part in leading bandits to extort and should be handed over for trial. The High Court also ordered the county to send police to Suzhou on the 17th to bring him back.

Exhaustion of Funds and Sale of Basic Property: Lu Lifan, Director of the Education Bureau, appointed Zhao Wudao as the Director of General Affairs on the 20th of Jiang. Due to the exhaustion of school funds, he tried every possible means to raise funds to pay two months' tuition fees in March, scheduled to be paid on the 20th, but there is still no way to pay for two and a half months. Director Lu and Director Zhao discussed that Nanwai has 108 mu of warehouse land as the basic educational property and sold it to the Chamber of Commerce Yin Zhongren and Yin Hengbai. The United Association of Teachers and Staff of the entire county heard the news yesterday and strongly opposed it.

Rugao 78

Continuation of the Bandit Attack on Shizhuang: Shizhuang Town in Rugao was attacked by thousands of bandits on the 11th. The county police and the security regiment fought bravely and defeated them. It is now learned that Squad Leader Tang Dongru and others took the lead, causing Tang's kidney to be injured, and the seventh squad leader Liu Huan died in battle. Among the policemen, Huang Kewen died in battle, and four other policemen were injured. The burnt houses are located in Dongxi Wangzhuang, Laobadou, and other places, as well as the salt stacks, the anti-smuggling battalion, and many families of the Shi and Min surnames in Henan.

Investigation of Liu Changyan's Private Release of Zhang Guangfeng: Liu Changyan, the former county chief of the county, privately released Zhang Zhaofeng, a local clearing supervisor of Matang who had been detained for shooting and wounding people (Zhang was Liu's private friend) when he was leaving office. The provincial government has been accused of this. The provincial government now considers it illegal and has decided to hand it over to the court for handling. Liu heard the news and was afraid of being punished and has been sending telegrams to various parties to provide excuses and confuse the situation to avoid heavy responsibilities, but the facts are all there and he may eventually be unable to escape the law.

Jiashan 79

Water Police and Bandit Gang Engage in Fierce Battle: The Jiashan Water Police Patrol Team encountered hundreds of bandits in more than 30 ships near Fanbang Town near Qingliang'an on the afternoon of the 14th. The two sides engaged in a fierce battle. The bandits gradually retreated and were on the verge of collapse at Yujiahui and scattered and fled. Eight bandit ships were intercepted by the water police, and one villager was killed and one injured by stray bullets.

Dispute over Deposits in Fengjing Fire Brigade: Since its establishment, all expenses and deposits of the Fengjing South City Fire Brigade have been deposited with Committee Member Zhang Tinghua. Later, a dispute arose because members wanted to withdraw the money. County Chief Shen sent personnel to mediate on the 15th and transferred the money to the Public Security Bureau to resolve the issue.

Hangzhou 80

Abolition of County and District Fund Associations: Zhu Jiahua, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Civil Affairs Office, returned to Hangzhou from Beijing yesterday. Since the autonomous regions of the counties have been prepared, the district offices of the districts are urgently waiting to be established within the time limit, but the problem of funding is difficult to solve. After careful deliberation, it was decided to abolish the fund associations of the counties and districts and transfer all the funds to the district offices to take over, and set up another supervisory committee to supervise them.

Sha Xian Representatives Arrive in Hangzhou to Plead: Since the seven counties in Jiaxing, Zhejiang changed the yarn donation to be collected by the unified donation bureau, the donation rate has increased and it is difficult for merchants to bear. More than 30 merchants, including Zhu Rongbo, were elected to prepare to petition for a reduction. The representatives arrived in Hangzhou yesterday and it is reported that they will petition the provincial government and the Ministry of Finance this morning (17th).

Wenzhou Wine Industry in Dire Straits: According to a wine merchant from Wenzhou, the wine industry in Wenzhou is in dire straits due to frequent disasters and bandits, rising rice prices, and a shortage of raw materials. The number of breweries that have stopped brewing this year is almost half that of last year, and unemployment among merchants has become a problem. It is estimated that there were 691 breweries last year, but only 324 this year.

Shaoxing 81

Request to Release Detained Cloth: When the first Shaoxing National Goods Exhibition opened, the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company transported 20 boxes of national goods cloth to Shaoxing to participate. The cloth was detained by the Cloth Donation Bureau in Nanxingqiao. After repeated requests for release, there was no effect. Recently, due to the humid weather and the risk of mold, the National Goods Promotion Association supplemented the tax exemption procedures and submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to issue a tax exemption certificate. Yesterday, a special representative was elected to go to Hangzhou to request the Ministry of Finance to approve the release of the cloth for inspection first.

Discuss Handling Pingtiao: The Shaoxing Grain and Miscellaneous Association convened a general meeting on the afternoon of the 17th to discuss solutions because problems such as handling Pingtiao need to be resolved.

Receipt Situation After the Termination of the Cocoon Donation Bureau: This year, 18 cocoon dealers in Shaoxing collected 209,000 kilograms of dry cocoons, yielding 18,800 yuan in cocoon donations. The bureau has reported to the Ministry of Finance after its termination yesterday.

Shangyu 82

Suspect in the Yangcun Murder Case Apprehended: Jin Tianchang, a resident of Yangcun, Xiejiatang District, Beixiang, had a dispute with his disciple Zi Mao on the afternoon of the 4th and was beaten by Xie Shen, Zi Mao's concubine, and his friend Yang Yongchao. Tianchang's body was suddenly found in a nearby river on the morning of the 5th. The Songxia Public Security Branch sent police to apprehend Tian Mao and Xie Shen and send them to the county government. On the 6th, Reviewing Officer Zhu went to the scene of the incident to verify the body. Since Yang Yongchao was on the run, the police were ordered to apprehend him. Unexpectedly, Yang Yongchao suddenly delivered a plea to the county government's receiving and dispatching office on the afternoon of the 12th and was arrested on the spot by the bailiff. Reviewing Officer Ting questioned Yang, and Yang's statements were ambiguous. He was ordered to be detained for investigation and continued interrogation.

Continuation of the School Building Collapse Injuring Five People: The school principal, Lin Chengson, reported to the Education Bureau after the incident of the sudden collapse of the three flat-roofed classrooms of the first-grade classroom of the fourth elementary school in Xiaoyue County on the afternoon of the 2nd, injuring five students, including Chen Zimao and school worker Yao Zhaozhu. The bureau sent Supervisor Qian Yu and Education Officer Zhu Shaoguang to the school to investigate and found that the entire school building was old and dilapidated and in disrepair for a long time. The injured students and school workers were sent to Fujih Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injuries were not life-threatening. However, the students' families feared that the remaining classrooms would suffer the same fate and asked for leave for their children, causing classes to be suspended for several days. It is now learned that the school, in order to avoid delaying the studies of the students, hired workers to repair the collapsed house first and resumed classes on the 14th. County Chief and Director of Education jointly sent letters to the initiators, scheduled to meet and discuss fundraising to rebuild the school.

Yueqing 83

Yueqing in Deep Water and Fire: The disasters in Yueqing are unprecedented in a century. The people are suffering from hunger and cold, and unexpectedly, they are also plagued by bandits. It is the most miserable situation. The people of Hongqiao District in the county have petitioned the provincial government to report the rampant bandits and the situation is quite painful. It is briefly mentioned that Yueqing is unfortunate to have suffered this great famine year and has also encountered banditry. Over the months, the National Defense Army has been carrying out repeated rounds of suppression of mountain bandits through Hongqiao, resulting in huge supplies, and it is difficult for local public funds and merchants to borrow and manage the high prices of rice and firewood. Since the National Army was invited to suppress bandits, a total of more than 1,300 yuan in food and other expenses has been spent. The main street of Hongqiao has repeatedly solicited donations, but only received about 400 yuan. There is no way to borrow the lost amount and we are just waiting to die. It is unbearable to have this kind of state. In addition, the main street of Hongqiao must raise funds to maintain public order for the militia group, and the amount needed is huge. It is impossible to donate one donation at a time. Commerce is declining and the people are not living. What's more, the National Army occasionally passes through one or two companies, and each time it passes through and stays for one night, it is impossible to handle the provision of food for breakfast and dinner without 130 to 40 yuan, and we are waiting to die with our hands tied like this and the people are getting tired to no end, and the street citizens' minds and resources are exhausted to the point of failure. In the event of our inability to do anything, then people will each seek escape for their persons, and the state of disarray in the place will be insufferable.

Relief Measures for Jurong Education Expenses 88

Previously, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, noting that Jurong County's education finances had accumulated deficits over the years to an irreparable state, had submitted a request to the provincial government to propose a committee meeting to consider the special circumstances of the county and provide relief. The provincial government instructed that the case be reported, and the government committee decided at its 300th meeting to instruct the finance department to allocate as much as possible under the provincial funds, and for the education and finance bureaus to jointly handle the county's school property to cope with the situation. In addition to recording the case and ordering the finance department to implement it, it is hoped that the county's education expenses can be eased.

Ministry of Education Retention

Luo Jialun, President of Tsinghua University 89

Mr. Luo's resignation is still very firm.

(National News Agency) Luo Jialun, president of National Tsinghua University, suddenly submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Education on May 23. Luo has made remarkable achievements in organizing Tsinghua and its construction over the past two years, and he has always been known for his sense of responsibility. His sudden resignation has attracted great attention from those concerned about education issues. There are not many complete universities in the country, and it is regrettable that Tsinghua, which has been put back on track, has suddenly experienced twists and turns. As for the agitation of a small number of students at this time, its background is worthy of consideration. Important documents regarding this matter are presented below.

Luo's original resignation request: "Submitting a request for resignation due to the deteriorating academic atmosphere. I, Jialun, was appointed to head Tsinghua nearly two years ago, and have made initial progress in organizing and constructing it. In these turbulent times, I have worked hard to maintain the vitality of national education. However, on May 20, the Student Union Congress had students proposing motions related to the president's retention. On the 21st, the motion was rejected by the majority of the entire student body. Although such phenomena are commonly seen and not surprising in the present day, it is not what I, Jialun, who has devoted myself to developing and expecting the most from Tsinghua, wish to see. I think it is due to a lack of trust. Although this motion was rejected by the congress, it shows that reason is in the hearts of the people, and there are many students who understand reason and care for scholarship. Moreover, I, Jialun, was appointed by the Party and the state and am directly under the Ministry. I know where I belong. However, such phenomena cannot but be said to be a sign of the deteriorating academic atmosphere. I believe that although the academic atmosphere is deteriorating, the morale must not be lost. Therefore, I earnestly request the Ministry to approve my resignation and appoint another capable person. I am deeply grateful. During this period of resignation, all school affairs will be handled by the school affairs meeting. I submit this together for your consideration." Jiang, Minister of Education, noted: "Mr. Luo's resignation was telegraphed on May 23. After its publication, he left the school. This resignation is a moral protest, fundamentally denying students the right to participate in the president's retention. In the current environment in Beiping, it is impossible to rectify the academic atmosphere, so he has taken this decisive step of withdrawal to let them recognize this as a matter of the integrity of the educator."

The Ministry of Education's original telegram of retention: After receiving Mr. Luo's resignation telegram, the Ministry of Education immediately sent telegrams on the 26th to retain Mr. Luo himself and the school affairs meeting. The original text is as follows: (To Mr. Luo) "Respectfully, Mr. Luo, President of National Tsinghua University, I have received your telegram. Organizing school affairs requires perseverance. I hope you will maintain your original aspirations, endure hardships, and not consider resigning. Sincerely, the Ministry of Education." (To the School Affairs Meeting) "Respectfully, the School Affairs Meeting of National Tsinghua University, I have received your telegram. The Ministry of Education has sent a special telegram to retain President Luo. I hope you will jointly persuade him. Before President Luo resumes his duties, please maintain all school affairs for the time being. Sincerely, the Ministry of Education."

Luo's Resignation Is Firm: After receiving the Ministry of Education's telegram, Luo believed that rectifying the academic atmosphere was not allowed by the current environment, and he was unwilling to carry on superficially if he could not rectify it. Therefore, he left Beiping on June 7 with a very firm intention to resign, it is said.

Ministry Order to Submit Revised Books for Review 90

The Ministry of Education stipulates that all books that are approved for review after revision must be submitted for review within a limited time, and a circular is issued to the provincial and municipal education departments and bureaus for compliance. The order reads:

"It has been found that many publishers have not submitted the revised versions of various books 'approved for review after revision' according to previous orders issued by the Ministry. Some have even submitted them after a long delay, which has caused many drawbacks. It is now stipulated that all books 'approved for review after revision' must be submitted for review within six months from the date of issuance of the order. Those who fail to submit the revised version within the deadline will have their original approval invalidated. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued for compliance."

Educational Institutions Not Allowed to Abuse Automobiles 91

The Ministry of Education, upon order, transmits an instruction to all educational institutions that they are not allowed to use automobiles excessively for non-official purposes in order to reduce consumption, it is said.

Shandong Provincial Educational Achievement Exhibition 92

Jinan Communication: The Shandong Provincial Educational Achievement Exhibition, which has been in preparation for a long time, opened at 10 a.m. on the 11th at the Shandong Provincial People's Education Hall. This is the first achievement exhibition since the implementation of the Three People's Principles education in the province, and the education community attaches great importance to it. The situation is recorded below: Exhibition Items: Inside the gate of the venue, to the west, is the Health Exhibition Hall. In the center is the Revolutionary Memorial Hall. In addition to various revolutionary memorabilia, there are also various photos of the May 3rd Massacre, in which the Japanese bombarded Jinan, and photos of the May 3rd Massacre Memorial碑 established by the Education Department in various counties throughout the province, which are most striking. From here, turning northwest, the road is marked with five-color paper tied with ropes. The sales office of the People's Education Hall is located on the west side of the road, and behind it is the venue. The downstairs in the northeast corner of the venue is the first room for the exhibition of scientific achievements, and the upstairs is the second room. The rooms display various achievements in natural science, social science, and language science. To the west is the first room for the vocational achievement exhibition. The first room contains many scientific instruments, the second room contains many woven fabrics, and the third room contains many leathers. Turning south is the art achievement exhibition hall. From north to south, the fourth room contains many woven fabrics, the third room contains many calligraphy and paintings, the second room contains various seals, and the first room contains woodwork, bamboo work, leather work, plaster work, etc., with no shortage of exquisite items. Further south are the World Book Company, Commercial Press, China Book Company, and educational supplies display areas. Further south is the exit.

Opening Ceremony: The opening ceremony was held at 10 o'clock as scheduled. He Siyuan, Director of the Education Department, presided over the meeting. Yan Qizhong and Li Xiawen were the recorders, and Zhang Yixian was the master of ceremonies. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of the opening, stating that today is the opening day of the Shandong Provincial Educational Achievement Exhibition. The province has been under the blue-white flag for two years. In the first year, due to diplomatic relations, the provincial government was located in a remote corner, and the education of the province could not be organized. In the past year, we have begun to organize and the results are not good, but relatively fast. During the Zhang Zongchang era, the province's education expenditure was only 1.3 million yuan per year, but now it has increased to 2.2 million yuan. Only with a stable economy can schools be sound and produce results for society to see. This national education conference was surprised by the speed of Shandong's education reorganization. With the exception of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Guangdong, Shandong has the most education funding of any province in the country. This is the result of the efforts of colleagues in the province's education community over the past year. It is hoped that we will continue to work hard. Education funding for the 19th year has increased to 2.82 million. The salaries of teachers at the province's first experimental primary school are higher than those of schools in Nanjing. Although several vocational schools were merged in the 19th year, 10 classes of rural teachers, 7 classes of junior high school, and 4 classes of senior high school were added. The current exhibition lacks achievements in compulsory education and rural teachers. It is now planned that by the 21st year, each large county will have a rural normal school, and every three small counties will have a rural normal school, with the rural normal school in the provincial capital as a model, and another rural normal school training class will be established to train teachers. In terms of compulsory education, Jinan and Yantai are designated as two compulsory education experimental zones. Preparatory committees have now been established. The six departments of the provincial government and the higher court will deduct 1/10 of their expenses to extract 200,000 yuan for Jinan's compulsory education expenses. There are only more than 30,000 school-age children in Jinan. It is planned to run 600 primary school classes over a two-year period, so that all children in Jinan can receive education. There is currently no compulsory education experimental zone in the country, and our province is the first to set an example. Recently, with the continuous artillery fire, all sectors have been able to maintain a calm attitude to visit and attend the meeting, and it is hoped that they will publicize it. Zhang Hanying and Qin Qirong, representatives of the Provincial Rectification Committee, and Wang Houzhi, representative of the Provincial Government, spoke as guests. Finally, Wang Shulin, Director of the Third Section of the Education Department, reported on the preparation process, stating that the exhibition is roughly divided into two major groups: education administration achievements and school achievements. The administrative achievements are limited to the Education Department and provincial schools, and the school achievements were received from 85 or 6 counties due to the current situation. All preparations and arrangements are also due to limited funds and the current situation, which is very imperfect and regrettable. A group photo was taken and the meeting adjourned. The public tour began at 1 p.m.

Local News

Recovering Concession Educational Rights 93

The petition of more than 30 schools such as Minli: Chen Jicheng, the principal of Shanghai Private School's Kindergarten Normal School, Su Yingjie of Minli Middle School, Tang Naikang of Shibei Middle School, Wang Suben of Minli Girls' Middle School, Yan Yucun Middle School, Wang Zhenshen of Yucun Middle School, Ling Zushou of Nanyang Girls' Middle School, and the principals of more than 30 other schools, yesterday submitted a petition to the Municipal Education Bureau, stating: "Submitting a petition to your bureau to quickly recover the educational rights of the concessions in order to uphold national rights and value culture. All countries in the world attach importance to education, because education is closely related to culture and national destiny, and should not be neglected. Today, the education in the Shanghai concessions is not under the jurisdiction of your bureau, but is controlled by the concession authorities, who arbitrarily impose colonial education on our country. The imperialists see this as a good strategy because they harbor the ambition to invade our culture. However, what about the future of education in our country? What about the culture and national destiny of our country? The principals of these schools are pained by the deprivation of educational rights and the transformation of national character, and cannot remain silent. They dare to cry out, hoping that the director will understand the situation and quickly negotiate with the concession authorities to recover the educational rights of the concessions, and will not stop until the goal is achieved."

Declaration of the Shanghai South District Education Association 94

The Shanghai Special Municipality South District Education Association yesterday solemnly issued a declaration on the recovery of the educational rights of the Shanghai concessions (excerpt): "The educational rights of the Shanghai concessions should be completely transferred to the Shanghai Special Education Bureau for unified facilities and increased efficiency. It is absolutely unnecessary for Chinese to overstep their authority. Then, the educational administrative power can be unified, the principle of Chinese people running Chinese education can be implemented, the millions of oppressed people in the concessions can be saved, and all anti-education facts in the concessions that can affect the whole country can be eliminated. Only then can the independent spirit of our Republic of China's thought and national culture be promoted and developed." (end of excerpt)

Shanghai Universities

Military Education Review of Achievements 95

Labor University and Jinan University are the best.

The military education of Shanghai universities has been reviewed by reviewing officers. According to reports, the results of this review showed that the achievements of the Agricultural College of Labor University were the best. The students of the college were divided into three classes, which were organized into one platoon according to the classes. The class leaders and platoon leaders were all students. During the drill, the company was coached by instructor Teng Qi. All students were able to accurately obey the commands of the instructor and class leaders. The movements were swift and orderly, and a courageous spirit was full of the spirit of fighting the enemy. The most commendable thing was that the students listened quietly to the remarks after the exercise for more than an hour without coughing and without fatigue. This kind of obedience is really hard to come by in schools and can be said to have a military spirit. The other schools may have neat steps but lack flexible movements, or they may have strict discipline but lack enthusiasm. They still cannot understand the meaning of commands and orders, so the movements are often inaccurate and cannot meet the requirements of the exercises and show their spirit of fighting the enemy. However, the rain drill at Jinan University shows a spirit of disregard for danger. This is the result of the review in terms of technical subjects. There are other aspects, such as the attitude of listening to lectures, the methods of teaching by instructors, etc., which have their own advantages, it is said.

Minutes of the Shanghai County Education Bureau's Bureau Affairs Meeting 96

The Shanghai County Education and Commerce Bureau held its 156th memorial week and bureau affairs meeting yesterday. The attendees were Director Shi, Supervisor Zhu, Zheng Guozhai, Sun Tingfang, Yang Huiming, Yan Chongguang, Xi Siwu, Yao Xingshu, Wu Renda, Pan Xingsan, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, and Yao Lanmi. Director Shi chaired the meeting and Pan Xingsan recorded. After the ceremonial procedures, a brief report was given, followed by discussion items: (1) A letter from the Municipal Land Bureau requesting the use of the Municipal Government Road Airfield to build a vehicle factory. It was resolved that in addition to requesting detailed addresses and application areas in the letter, it would be submitted to the Administrative Committee for discussion. (2) The county magistrate reviewed the Municipal Government's notification to stop Meixi Primary School, and the bureau's land rent will be transferred to the city. It was resolved that the matter concerned the bureau's property rights and should be submitted to the Administrative Committee for discussion. (3) The radio station negotiated the rental of houses near Panfang. It was resolved to send someone to negotiate. (4) The county magistrate re-revised the Shanghai County Education and Property Management Committee Regulations. It was resolved to revise and pass. (5) The construction of the Zhenxin Primary School building has been completed and a request was made to send someone to inspect and accept it. It was resolved to order the principal to prepare detailed final accounts, together with two copies of the school building drawings, to be submitted for approval by the county and sent for inspection and acceptance. (6) The date of the summer Administrative Committee meeting was decided to be 1 p.m. on June 22. (7) The Regulations of the Public Education Committee were discussed and it was resolved to revise the letter, pass it, and submit it for record. (8) The County Education Association submitted a request to hold a summer seminar. It was resolved that the School Education Section would plan it before further discussion. (9) A department order was issued to recommend students to attend the summer school of the People's Education Institute and the Labor and Agriculture Institute. It was resolved that, in addition to the bureau's staff, Jin Zuobin, Zhang Yi, and Zhang Qiao, the directors of the social education institutions, should be designated to prepare procedures to be recommended by the bureau. The meeting adjourned immediately after the discussion.

Record of the Changming Art School Painting Exhibition 100

The Changming Art School Painting Exhibition on Belle Road was on its second day (Sunday) yesterday. The weather was sunny in the morning, and visitors came in an endless stream. The author arrived at the venue at 11 o'clock and saw that there were no less than 400 pieces of work in total. Chinese paintings accounted for 80 or 90 percent, displayed on all four walls and in the corridors of the stairs, with almost no space left. The paintings were dazzling and beautiful. Wang Yiting's "Hanshan and Shide" vividly depicted the expressions and charm. Wu Dongmai and Zhu Le's calligraphy had deep skills. Zhu Wenyun's "Several Dynasty Pictures" had elegant colors and a natural ink pine charm. Wang Geyi's "Escape from the Sky" was painted with extraordinary brushstrokes. Students such as Feng Jianwu, Hua Bonian, Zhang Weiwen, Wu Yaohua, and Li Yantao were all able to have their own characteristics and strengths in fine brushwork and sketching. The calligraphy of female student Shen Yunzhen was also delicate and lovely. In addition, there were many other works by Gui Zuo Shang, which could not be recorded in detail. It is heard that the school will add a Western painting department next semester, melting Chinese and Western art in one furnace, and its progress can be predicted.
